    INNER JOIN [Produits] AS [p] ON [d2].[ProduitId] = [p].[Id]
) AS [t2] ON [t].[Id] = [t2].[DemandeId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t].[Id2], [t].[Id3], [t].[Id4], [t0].[CreatedDate] DESC, [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [t2].[Id]" (0723d8ff)
